Set the following number to 10000 if you wish to enable a meaningful numerical approximatins to integrals.
Set it to something smaller than 10 if you wish to completely disable numerical approximations for integrals. If this
is disabled, then the website will only evaluate the integrals of polynomials. This parameter mostly affects the queries
submitted through the Calculator form.

_vVPair__vr_<p>Help with rules</p>_/vr__vl_
<h4>Make grading easier with custom rules and policies</h4>
_hideReveal__revealTitle_Show details_/revealTitle__hideTitle_Hide details_/hideTitle_
<h5>Adding a rule</h5>
<p>Let us show an example of a custom rule called <code>pineapple</code>. A rule can be added by inserting the command below into the comment
section of a problem that is being graded.</p>
<pre>[add]pineapple;
-3;
<p>Your solution contains a recipe that adds pineapple to a pizza.
This is really bad.
Three points will be deducted from your score.</p>
[/add]</pre>
<p>The rule will be added to a table. The command will disappear from the comment section. </p>
<h5>Applying a rule</h5> <p>You can apply this rule for any of the students. Just write the following in the comment section: </p>
<pre>[r]pineapple[/r]</pre>
<p>The poor student will loose 3 points and receive the feedback specified with the rule.</p>
<h5>Changing a rule</h5>
<p>If you later change your mind, and decide that 5 points should be deducted instead of 3, then you need to add the command: </p>
<pre>[add]pineapple;
-5;
<p>Your solution contains a recipe that adds pineapple to a pizza.
This is really bad.
Five points will be deducted from your score.</p>
[/add]</pre>
<p>All students who were subject to the rule will have their score and the feedback changed.</p>
<h5>Deleting a rule</h5>
<p>If you want to delete a rule, then type the command:</p>
<pre>[delete]pineapple[/delete]</pre>
_/hideReveal_
<p></p>

<p></p><h2>Timed Exam</h2>
<p>The timer will be activated once the problems are displayed for solving. </p>
<p>You can change your answers as many times as you want before the expiration of the timer. After each change, you must click on the button with the label <b>Update / Save / Re-submit</b>.</p>
<p>If you are done before the expiration of the timer, make sure that you click on <b>Update / Save / Re-submit</b> one last time before closing the web browser.
</p>
<p>Click on the button below when you are ready.</p>_/vl__/vVPair_

_vVPair__vr_TimerJS_/vR__vl_ <div class="card bg-primary text-white">
    <div class="card-body">

<b><span id="gytimer"></span></b>

<script>
var maxTime = _|*tmSeconds*|_;
var end = new Date().getTime()+maxTime*1000;
var x = setInterval(function() {
  var now = new Date().getTime();
  var distance = end - now;
  var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
  var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
  var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
  var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);
  document.getElementById("gytimer").innerHTML = days + "d " + hours + "h "
  + minutes + "m " + seconds + "s ";
  if (distance < 0) {
    clearInterval(x);
    document.getElementById("gytimer").innerHTML = "Time is up!";
  }
}, 1000);
</script>

 <H3>Command: Backup with Range</H3>

_insert_
_n*_formInitialization_/n*_
_n*_reqCommand_/n*_
_n*_index.cgi?comEx=yes_/n*_
_/insert_


_insert_
_n*_textAreaField_/n*_
_n*_reqCommand_/n*_
_n*_commands_/n*_
_n*_The command is pre-filled with some parameters. You should list the range of the id numbers of texts that you want to backup. The first number <code>alpha</code> is the start of the range. The second number <code>beta</code> is the end of the range. The site will backup all documents whose index is $\geq$ <code>alpha</code> and $\lneq$ <code>beta</code>. The output will be a text document that consists of commands. The execution of the commands will put the saved texts to the database._/n*_
_n*_DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _command_
DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _nc***_backup_/nc***_
DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _nc***_Texts_/nc***_
EDIT AFTER THE SYMBOL -----> _nc***_
_n*!_range_/n*!_
_n*!_alpha_/n*!_
_n*!_beta_/n*!_
_/nc***_ <-----  STOP EDITING AFTER THIS SYMBOL
DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _/command__/n*_

 <H3>Command: Assign Graders</H3>

_insert_
_n*_formInitialization_/n*_
_n*_reqCommand_/n*_
_n*_index.cgi?comEx=yes_/n*_
_/insert_


_insert_
_n*_textAreaField_/n*_
_n*_reqCommand_/n*_
_n*_commands_/n*_
_n*_The course created from one of the <a href="?page=administratorMain">templates</a> will have custom buttons and links to assign graders. This raw version of the command should probably never be used. Instead of listing the graders explicitly, you can replace the text with a single letter <code>a</code> or a single letter <code>s</code>. The obtained parameter will look like <code>_nc!verbSave!***_a__nc!verbSave!***_</code> or <code>_nc!verbSave!***_s__nc!verbSave!***_</code>. The code <code>a</code> means that all students will become graders. The exams will be randomly distributed among themselves. Nobody would know who is their grader. The students will also not know whose exam they are grading. The code <code>s</code> means that each student will self-grade their own work._/n*_
_n*_DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _command_
DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _nc***_assignGraders_/nc***_
LINE TO EDIT                       -----> _nc***_examResponseReceiverCode_/nc***_
EDIT AFTER THE SYMBOL -----> _nc***_

_n*_userNameOfGrader1_/n*_
_n*_userNameOfGrader2_/n*_
_n*_userNameOfGrader3_/n*_

_/nc***_ <-----  STOP EDITING AFTER THIS SYMBOL
DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _/command__/n*_
_/insert_

 <H3>Command: Create Another Website</H3>

_insert_
_n*_formInitialization_/n*_
_n*_reqCommand_/n*_
_n*_index.cgi?comEx=yes_/n*_
_/insert_


_insert_
_n*_textAreaField_/n*_
_n*_reqCommand_/n*_
_n*_commands_/n*_
_n*_This command works only if the website allows cloning. If there is a member with username <code>mathLessons</code>, and this username is put in the command, then the new website will be created at the subdomain <code>sites/mathLessons</code>. The new site will start as empty with initializing texts only. The administrator will be <code>mathLessons</code>. The initial password will be the same as the one that <code>mathLessons</code> had here at the time when the command was executed. If the website <code>sites/mathLessons</code> already exists, then the command will delete it first and then create a new one. _/n*_
_n*_DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _command_
DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _nc***_createWebsiteForUser_/nc***_
LINE TO EDIT                       -----> _nc***_userName_/nc***_
DO NOT EDIT THIS LINE     -----> _/command__/n*_
_/insert_

<table class="table table-striped">

<th>Category</th>
</tr>
 </thead><tbody>

<tr><td><A href="index.cgi?page=listResponses">Response Receivers</A></td><td>Automatic 1</td></tr>
<tr><td><A href="index.cgi?page=listOfForms">Forms</A></td><td>Automatic 1</td></tr>
<tr><td> <A href="index.cgi?page=listUsers">Users</A></td><td>Automatic 1</td></tr>
<tr><td> <A href="index.cgi?page=listCoursesAndAssignments">Courses and Assignments</A></td><td>Automatic 2</td></tr>
<tr><td> <A href="index.cgi?page=listCertificates">Certificates</A></td><td>Automatic 2</td></tr>
<tr><td><A href="index.cgi?page=listMessages">Messages</A></td><td>Automatic 3</td></tr>
<tr><td><A href="index.cgi?page=listFiles">Files</A></td><td>Automatic 3</td></tr>
<tr><td><A href="index.cgi?page=listStat">Statistics</A></td><td>Automatic 3</td></tr>
<tr><td><A href="index.cgi?page=listBackups">Restore from Backup</A></td><td>Automatic 3</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div>
<ul>
<li><b>Manual</b> database(s) are edited frequently by the administrator. </li>
<li><b>Automatic 1</b> database(s) are sometimes accessed directly and edited by the administrator. </li>
<li><b>Automatic 2</b> rarely need to be accessed by administrators. The robot is supposed to be fairly good at maintaining these databases.</li>
<li><b>Automatic 3</b> category means that the robots should be doing everything. </li>
</ul>
</div>

<p></p>
<h2>Mass enrollment</h2>
<p>This code can be used to add students to the course. The database of students can be harvested from the CUNYfirst portal. It is sufficient to copy and paste the content displayed html. Make sure to include the entire table and little bit of text before and after the table (the algorithm will figure out where are the students and their CUNY ids). In the end, you need to add the email addresses of the students (separated by commas). They can be obtained from the link "notify all students". Example of the command is shown below </p>
_hideReveal__revealTitle_Show code_/revealTitle__hideTitle_Hide code_/hideTitle_

<h2>Generate exam</h2>
<p>This code will create the exam in the database _cde_responceReceiver_/cde_.</p>
_hideReveal__revealTitle_Show code_/revealTitle__hideTitle_Hide code_/hideTitle_
_codeBox_
_command_
_nc***_generateExam_/nc***_
_nc***_MTH000M1Problems_/nc***_
_nc***_
_examOptions*|_

***************************************************
***                MAIN SETUP OF THE EXAM             ***
***************************************************



***************************************************
***                SECTION 1: EXAM STATUS              ***
***************************************************
****************       _sf*|_n_/sf*|_      **************
***************************************************

Status is one of the following: n/a/q/s/c/sc/p/sp
 n - not available. Exam is closed and questions are not shown
 a - active. Exam is open and students can submit responses to questions
 q - exam is closed for answering.
         The questions and responses are displayed
 s - exam is closed for answering.
         The questions, responses, and official answers are displayed

 p - exam is closed for answering.
         The questions, responses, and points from the grader are displayed.
 sp - exam is closed for answering.
         The questions, responses, points, and official solutions are displayed.

 c - exam is closed for answering.
         The questions, responses, points, and the comments by the grader are displayed.
 sc - exam is closed for answering.
         The questions, responses, points, grader's comments, and official solutions are displayed.


***************************************************
***            SECTION 2: GRADING STATUS            ***
***************************************************
**************       _sgr*|_n_/sgr*|_      *************
***************************************************

Status is one of the following: n/a/
 n - not available. Grading is closed and nothing is shown to the grader
 a - active. Grades can be submitted by the grader.



***************************************************
*** SECTION 3: LABEL ON THE SUBMIT BUTTON ***
***************************************************

***************************************************

<h3>In-person exams with only auto-grader support and no displayed questions</h3>
<p>Follow the two steps to edit the section between tags <code>_problems*|_</code> and <code>_/problems*|_</code>:</p>
<ul><li><b>Step 1.</b> Remove the individual problems (the components between tags <code>_in*|_</code> and <code>_/in*|_</code>;
</li><li><b>Step 2.</b> Put a modification of the document:
<pre>_noDisplayProblems|_
Points assigned to problems: _pt*|_5;5;5;5;10;10;10_/pt*|_
Answers to version 0: _n*_E;E;A;D;17;28;31_/n*_
Answers to version 1: _n*_B;A;E;C;27;$\frac{1}{3}$;19_/n*_
Answers to version 2:_n*_C;E;E;A;$x^2$;-17;29_/n*_
_/noDisplayProblems|_</pre>
The number of versions does not have to be 3. The number of problems does not have to be 7. However, it would be the best if each version has equal number of problems. Otherwise, you have to read the source code to see what will happen. When the parameters are badly broken (like unequal numbers of problems in different versions of the exams), then the program will do everything to prevent segmentation fault. The comfort of the administrator who made the bad parameters will be the least of the program's concern.
</li>
</ul>
_/textData!!_

students whose assignments you want to customize. Replace the
number 0 with an appropriate version number.

You can add student's answers as well. After the version parameter,
you can add

_ans*_B;E;;A;A_/ans*_

This will set the answers to the questions
1, 2, 4, and 5. The answers will be set to 1:B, 2:E, 4:A, 5:A

_tx*|_ Evaluate $\frac{{x1}+{x2}\cdot{x3}}{{den}}$.
_/tx*|_




_sl*|_We first evaluate the numerator and obtain ${x1}+{x2}\cdot {x3}={num}$. Thus the final answer is
\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{{x1}+{x2}\cdot{x3}}{{den}}=\frac{{num}}{{den}}={answer}.
\end{eqnarray*}
_/sl*|_

_tx*|_  <p>Create a C++ program that reads two integers $x$ and $y$ from user input and calculates ${alpha}x + {beta}y+{alpha+beta}$.
</p>

<p>You should not use sequences, arrays, or any commands that include this symbol: $[$ </p>
_/tx*|_




_sl*|_ <p>This is an easy problem that illustrates how to use the automatic code grader. The performance of the code submitted by the student will be compared to the performance of the code in the official solution. Student's solution and official solution can contain explanation in addition to the code that will be compiled and executed. The last code block of the student solution and the last code block of the official solution will be sent to the auto-grader. The other code blocks will be ignored. Each code will be executed on the specified test cases. For each of the test cases, the student will receive points if the output of his/her code is the same as the output of the official code. Test cases can have different numbers of points assigned to them. </p>
<p>This is a code in the official solution that will be ignored: <pre>code to ignore;
It is even incorrect;
int x=8;//the only correct line in my code.
</pre>
</p>

<p>It is important to note that as a safety precausion <code>#include<???></code> commands will be commented out by compiler both for the official solution and the student's submission. The official solution has to list the libraries that have to be included. The auto-grader will add those libraries instead of the ones that are commented out. In order to have a nicer exposition, I will include the <code>iostream</code> library in the beginning of my solution. However, even if I did not do that, the code would add this library.</p>
<p>And now, we will write the last code-block that will be sent to the auto-grader.  </p>
<pre>
#include<iostream>
int main(){
   int x; int y;
   std::cin>>x>>y;
   std::cout<<{alpha}*x+{beta}*y+{alpha+beta}<<std::endl;
   return 0;
}
</pre>
_/sl*|_

long sz=v.size();
if(sz<1){
   return -1;

   if({command}){
      m=v[i];
   }
}
return m;

_tx*|_  <p>Create a python program that reads two positive integers $x$ and $y$ from user input and calculates the number of integers in the interval $[x,x+y]$ that are divisible by ${alpha}$. The integers $x$ and $y$ are provided in a single line and they are separated by a space character. You can input these two integers with the command:
<pre>
x, y = map(int, input().split())
</pre>
</p>

_/tx*|_




_sl*|_ <p>This is an easy problem that illustrates how to use the automatic code grader. The performance of the code submitted by the student will be compared to the performance of the code in the official solution. Student's solution and official solution can contain explanation in addition to the code that will be compiled and executed. The last code block of the student solution and the last code block of the official solution will be sent to the auto-grader. The other code blocks will be ignored. Each code will be executed on the specified test cases. For each of the test cases, the student will receive points if the output of his/her code is the same as the output of the official code. Test cases can have different numbers of points assigned to them. </p>
<p>This is a code in the official solution that will be ignored: <pre>code to ignore;
It is even incorrect;
int x=8 #the only correct line in my code.
</pre>
</p>

<p>It is important to note that as a safety precaution <code>import ???</code> commands will be commented out before execution both for the official solution and the student's submission. The official solution has to list the libraries that have to be imported. The auto-grader will add those libraries instead of the ones that are commented out. </p>
<p>And now, we will write the last code-block that will be sent to the auto-grader.  </p>
<pre>
x, y = map(int, input().split())
smallestDivisibleNumber=x
while smallestDivisibleNumber % {alpha} !=0 :
	smallestDivisibleNumber += 1
largestDivisibleNumber=x+y
while largestDivisibleNumber % {alpha} !=0:
	largestDivisibleNumber -= 1
if largestDivisibleNumber < smallestDivisibleNumber:
	print(0)
else:
	print((largestDivisibleNumber-smallestDivisibleNumber) // {alpha} +1)
</pre>
_/sl*|_

<h2>_vr_aType_/vr_ _vr_aNum_/vr_  grading</h2>

_insert_
_n*_responseReceiverStatus_/n*_
_n*__vr_docName_/vr__vr_grExt_/vr__vr_aNP_/vr_p_/n*_
_/insert_

\begin{box}<p><b>The status table</b> </p><p> The symbol <span class="badge badge-pill bg-success">+</span> means that the corresponding category is active. The symbol <span class="badge badge-pill bg-danger">-</span> means that the category is not active. The abbreviations have the following meanings:
</p>
<ul><li><b>E:</b> Exam (or homework assignment). The status symbol shows whether the exam is open for students to solve.
</li>
<li><b>Q:</b> Questions. The status symbol shows whether the questions are visible to students (this category is always active if the category E is active). </li>
<li><b>S:</b> Solutions. The status symbol shows whether the solutions are visible to students (this category is always inactive if the category E is active. In other words, students cannot see the solutions at the time they are working on the assignment).</li>
<li><b>P:</b> Points.  The status symbol shows whether the students can see the points that they received.</li>
<li><b>C:</b> Comment.  The status symbol shows whether the students can see the comments that the instructor has left after grading.</li>
<li><b>G:</b> Grading.  The status symbol shows whether the assignment is open for grading. If it is not open, then the grading is not possible.</li>
<li><b>S:</b> Solutions.  The status symbol shows whether the grader can see the solutions. This one is always on, if the grading is open.</li>

</ul>
\end{box}

_n*_G Off_/n*_
_n*_index.cgi?r=_vr_docName_/vr__vr_grExt_/vr__vr_aNP_/vr_p&rdd=ch000n&fP=GrMain&fv0=docName&fl0=_vr_docName_/vr_&fv1=aType&fl1=_vr_aType_/vr_&fv2=aNum&fl2=_vr_aNum_/vr_&fv3=grExt&fl3=_vr_grExt_/vr_&fv4=aNP&fl4=_vr_aNP_/vr_&fv5=mRR&fl5=_vr_mRR_/vr__/n*_
_/insert_

</div>
\begin{box} <b>Main switch-board</b>
<ul>
<li><b>Off:</b> Emergency off button. Everything that can be turned off will be turned off. </li>
<li><b>E On:</b> Exam is turned on for solving. </li>
<li><b>E Off:</b> Exam is turned off. No solving, and no display of question or solutions.</li>
<li><b>E QA:</b> Exam is turned off. However, the following items are displayed: the exam questions, and the answers that the student submitted.</li>
<li><b>& Sol:</b> Exam is turned off. In addition to the exam questions and student's solutions, the student will also see the official solutions.</li>
<li><b>& Pts:</b> Exam is turned off. The students will see the exam questions, their submissions, the official solutios, and the points they received, if the exam was graded.</li>
<li><b>& Comments:</b> Exam is turned off. The students will see the exam questions, their submissions, the official solutios, the points they received, and the comments from the grader, if the exam was graded.</li>
</ul>
\end{box}
</div>

_n*_buttonLink_/n*_
_n*_Auto-grade_/n*_
_n*_index.cgi?r=_vr_docName_/vr__vr_grExt_/vr__vr_aNP_/vr_&rdd=gr&fP=GrMain&fv0=docName&fl0=_vr_docName_/vr_&fv1=aType&fl1=_vr_aType_/vr_&fv2=aNum&fl2=_vr_aNum_/vr_&fv3=grExt&fl3=_vr_grExt_/vr_&fv4=aNP&fl4=_vr_aNP_/vr_&fv5=mRR&fl5=_vr_mRR_/vr__/n*_
_/insert_
</div>
\begin{box}<b>Exam creation and customization</b>
<br><b>Warning:</b> It is not safe, nice, nor polite to use some of the operations in this category <b>after</b> the students have started working on the assignment.
<ul>
<li><b>Create:</b> If the exam is not created yet, this button will take you to the page where you can insert the problems and customize the parameters. If the exam already exists, you need to first delete the exam from the <code>Response Receiver</code> database before creating it again.</li>
<li><b>Backup:</b> Puts student answers in a form that can be used as a backup command and that can be used in offline grading tools.</li>
<li><b>CSV:</b> Displays data in CSV format.</li>
<li><b>Custom versions:</b> If there are multiple versions of problems, then the <code>Create</code> button would randomly assign the versions to students. The number of possible versions is unbounded. If you want to avoid that, then you should click on this button and adjust the settings to your liking.</li>
<li><b>PDF:</b> Create latex source file or pdf files with exam problems. </li>
<li><b>Graders:</b> Assign students to grade each other, or to self-grade their own work.</li>
<li><b>Timer:</b> Set up exam timers and deadlines.</li>
<li><b>Enroll:</b> Enroll additional users or guests to the exam. Exam links will be sufficient to access and solve the exam.</li>
<li><b>Auto-grade:</b> Use the auto grader to help you grade multiple-choice problems, problems that have very short answers, or computer science assignments in C++ and python. The autograder will read all of the problems from all of the students, and identify and grade several problems that it is capable of grading. <b>Note:</b> You may need to call the auto-grader multiple times to grade all of the computer codes. </li>
</ul>
\end{box}
</div>

<p></p>
\begin{box}
<h2>Math and Probability Calculator</h2>
<p><b>Pre-filled queries.</b> The input form can accept a wide variety of queries. By clicking on one of the buttons, the input field gets pre-filled with a relevant request. Then you can modify the request to get the desired answer.
</p>
<p><b>Calculator.</b> If you write a math formula that a simple calculator can evaluate, then you will see the end result of the calculation.  </p>
<p><b>Random sampling.</b> You can specify one of the available probability distributions, its parameters, and the number of samples that you want to have generated.
</p>
<p><b>Random permutations.</b> The program can also generate random permutations. You need to provide the smallest and the largest integer in the permutation. You can also ask for several permutations, and in that case you can ask whether you want them displayed horizontally or vertically.
</p>
\end{box}
<p></p>

 <H2>Math formulas</H2>
<p>Math formulas should be placed between the dollar symbols \(\$\). If you write \(\$\)_cde_x+\frac{7}{x^2+1}_/cde_\(\$\), then your submission will look like \(x+\frac{7}{x^2+1}\). </p>
<H2>Computer code</H2>
<p>This computer code should be placed between the words
</p>
<center> <img src="img/code_open.png" width="130" height="44"> and
<img src="img/code_close.png" width="130" height="44"></center>
<p>This is how a computer assignment should be answered.
</p><center>
<img src="img/typingSolutionWithCode.png" width="480" height="419">
 </center>
<p>After clicking on <code>Update/Save/Re-submit</code>, you will see the formatted code above the box in which you can further edit your submission.</p>
<center>
<img src="img/solutionTypedWithCode.png" width="480" height="649">
 </center>

<H2>Auto-grading of computer code</H2>
<p>If autograder is used, then it will only grade the <b>last</b> code in your submission. Your solution can contain explanation in words, and several blocks of code. If that is the case, then only the last one will be executed by the auto-grader. If you do not put anything between the code tags, then the autograder will assume that your entire solution is the code that you want to be graded. </p><p>If your code does not compile, the auto-grader will assign 0 points for that problem.</p>

function mPosition(e)
{
   var tX=0;
   var tY=0;
   while(e){
      tX += e.offsetLeft;
      tY += e.offsetTop;
      e=e.offsetParent;
    }
    return [tX,tY];
}

function imgAnalysis()
{
 var imgPos = mPosition(iForCoordinates);
 var cX = window.event.pageX - imgPos[0];

 document.getElementById("llxF19271").innerHTML = llX.toFixed(2);

}

#ifndef _INCL_STsetmap_CPP
#define _INCL_STsetmap_CPP

namespace ssm{
  template<typename KEY> class set{
  private:
    class AVLNode{
    public:
      KEY value;
      long leftCount;
      long rightCount;
      long height;
      AVLNode* leftChild;
      AVLNode* rightChild;
      AVLNode(){
        leftChild=nullptr;
        rightChild=nullptr;
        leftCount=-17;
        rightCount=-17;
      }
      AVLNode(const KEY& k ) {
        value = k; leftChild = nullptr;
        rightChild = nullptr;
        leftCount=-17;
        rightCount=-17;
        height = 1;
      }
    }* _dRoot;
    long _size;
    long getHeight(AVLNode * );
    long hDiff(AVLNode * );
    long redoHeight(AVLNode * );
    AVLNode* rRotation(AVLNode* );
    AVLNode* lRotation(AVLNode* );
    AVLNode* balance(AVLNode* );
    AVLNode* insertInTree(AVLNode* , const KEY & , long & );
    AVLNode* getMinNode(AVLNode* );
    AVLNode* rewireMin(AVLNode* );
    AVLNode* removeFromTree(AVLNode* , const KEY& , long & );
    AVLNode* duplicateTree(AVLNode*);
    void clearAVLTree(AVLNode*);
    KEY avl_access(AVLNode* , const long & ) const;
  public:
    set();
    set(const set &);
    set& operator=(const set &);
    set(set&&);
    set& operator=(set &&);
    long size() const;
    long erase(const KEY & );
    long erase(const set & );
    long insert(const KEY & );
    long insert(const set &);
    long operator+=(const KEY &);
    long operator+=(const set &);
    long operator-=(const KEY &);
    long operator-=(const set &);
    std::pair<long,KEY> findIK(const KEY &, const long & = 0) const;
    long find(const KEY &, const long & = 0) const;
    long upperBound(const KEY &) const;
    void clear();
    KEY operator[](const long & ) const;
    virtual ~set();
  };
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::getHeight(AVLNode * root){
    if(root==nullptr){
      return 0;
    }
    return root->height;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::hDiff(AVLNode * root){
    return getHeight(root->rightChild)-getHeight(root->leftChild);
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::redoHeight(AVLNode * root){
    long lHeight = getHeight(root->leftChild);
    long rHeight = getHeight(root->rightChild);
    root->height = rHeight;
    if(lHeight>rHeight){root->height = lHeight;}
    root->height += 1;
    return root->height;
  }
  template<typename KEY>
  typename set<KEY>::AVLNode* set<KEY>::rRotation(AVLNode * root){
    AVLNode * other = root->leftChild;
    root->leftChild = other->rightChild;
    other->rightChild = root;
    long a,c;
    a= other->leftCount;
    c= root->rightCount;
    root->leftCount -= (a+1);
    other->rightCount += (c+1);
    redoHeight(root);
    redoHeight(other);
    return other;
  }
  template<typename KEY>
  typename set<KEY>::AVLNode * set<KEY>::lRotation(AVLNode * root){
    AVLNode * other = root->rightChild;
    root->rightChild = other->leftChild;
    other->leftChild = root;
    long a,c;
    a= other->rightCount;
    c=root->leftCount;
    root->rightCount -= (a+1);
    other->leftCount += (c+1);
    redoHeight(root);
    redoHeight(other);
    return other;
  }
  template<typename KEY>
  typename set<KEY>::AVLNode * set<KEY>::
  balance(AVLNode * root){
    redoHeight(root);
    if( hDiff(root)==2 ){
      if( hDiff(root->rightChild) < 0 ){
        root->rightChild = rRotation(root->rightChild);
      }
      return lRotation(root);
    }
    if( hDiff(root)==-2 ){
      if( hDiff(root->leftChild) > 0 ){
        root->leftChild = lRotation(root->leftChild);
      }
      return rRotation(root);
    }
    return root;
  }
  template<typename KEY>
  typename set<KEY>::AVLNode * set<KEY>::
  insertInTree(AVLNode * root, const KEY & _value, long & insSucc){
    if( root==nullptr ){
      insSucc=1;
      AVLNode *fR=new AVLNode (_value);
      fR->leftCount=0;
      fR->rightCount=0;
      return fR;
    }
    if( _value < root->value ){
      root->leftChild = insertInTree(root->leftChild,_value,insSucc);
      if(insSucc==1){
        root->leftCount+=1;
      }
    }
    else{
      if(root->value < _value ){
        root->rightChild = insertInTree(root->rightChild,_value,insSucc);
        if(insSucc==1){
          root->rightCount+=1;
        }
      }
      else{
        insSucc=0;
        return root;
      }
    }
    if(insSucc==1){
      return balance(root);
    }
    return root;
  }
  template<typename KEY>
  typename set<KEY>::AVLNode * set<KEY>::getMinNode(AVLNode * root){
    if(root->leftChild==nullptr){
      return root;
    }
    return getMinNode(root->leftChild);
  }
  template<typename KEY>
  typename set<KEY>::AVLNode * set<KEY>::rewireMin(AVLNode * root){
    if( root->leftChild==nullptr ){
      return root->rightChild;
    }
    root->leftChild = rewireMin(root->leftChild);
    root->leftCount -= 1;
    return balance(root);
  }
  template<typename KEY>
  typename set<KEY>::AVLNode *
        set<KEY>::removeFromTree(AVLNode * root, const KEY& _value,
           long & remSucc){
    if( root==nullptr ){
      remSucc=0;
      return nullptr;
    }
    if( _value < root->value ){
      root->leftChild = removeFromTree(root->leftChild,_value, remSucc);
      if(remSucc==1){
        root->leftCount -=1;
      }
    }
    else{
      if(root->value < _value ){
        root->rightChild = removeFromTree(root->rightChild,_value,remSucc);
        if(remSucc==1){
          root->rightCount -=1;
        }
      }
      else{
        AVLNode * lTemp = root->leftChild;
        AVLNode * rTemp = root->rightChild;
        long oldleftCount,oldrightCount;
        oldleftCount=root->leftCount;
        oldrightCount=root->rightCount;
        delete root;
        remSucc=1;
        if( rTemp == nullptr ){
          return lTemp;
        }
        AVLNode * rightMin = getMinNode(rTemp);
        rightMin->rightChild = rewireMin(rTemp);
        rightMin->leftChild = lTemp;
        rightMin->leftCount=oldleftCount;
        rightMin->rightCount=oldrightCount-1;
        remSucc=1;
        return balance(rightMin);
      }
    }
    return balance(root);
  }
  template<typename KEY> void set<KEY>::clearAVLTree(AVLNode *root){
    if(root!=nullptr){
      clearAVLTree(root->leftChild);
      clearAVLTree(root->rightChild);
      delete root;
    }
    return;
  }
  template<typename KEY>
  typename set<KEY>::AVLNode *
     set<KEY>::duplicateTree(AVLNode *root){
    AVLNode *newN;
    newN=nullptr;
    if(root!=nullptr){
      newN=new AVLNode;
      newN->value=root->value;
      newN->leftCount=root->leftCount;
      newN->rightCount=root->rightCount;
      newN->height=root->height;
      newN->leftChild = duplicateTree(root->leftChild);
      newN->rightChild= duplicateTree(root->rightChild);
    }
    return newN;
  }
  template<typename KEY> KEY
   set<KEY>::avl_access(AVLNode *root, const long &i) const{
    if(root==nullptr){
      KEY tempWithRandValue;
      return tempWithRandValue;
    }
    if(i==root->leftCount){
      return root->value;
    }
    if(i<root->leftCount){
      return avl_access(root->leftChild,i);
    }
    return avl_access(root->rightChild, i-root->leftCount-1);
  }
  template<typename KEY> set<KEY>::set(){
    _dRoot=nullptr;
    _size=0;
  }
  template<typename KEY> set<KEY>::set(const set<KEY>& _copyFrom){
    _dRoot=nullptr;
    _dRoot= duplicateTree(_copyFrom._dRoot);
    _size= _copyFrom._size;
  }
  template<typename KEY> set<KEY>::set( set<KEY>&& _moveFrom){
    _size= _moveFrom._size;
    _moveFrom._size=0;
    _dRoot=_moveFrom._dRoot;
    _moveFrom._dRoot=nullptr;
  }
  template<typename KEY> set<KEY>&
    set<KEY>::operator=(const set<KEY>& _copyFrom){
    if(&_copyFrom!=this){
      clear();
      _dRoot= duplicateTree(_copyFrom._dRoot);
      _size= _copyFrom._size;
    }
    return *this;
  }
  template<typename KEY> set<KEY>&
     set<KEY>::operator=( set<KEY>&& _moveFrom){
    if(&_moveFrom!=this){
      clear();
      _size= _moveFrom._size;
      _dRoot= _moveFrom._dRoot;
      _moveFrom._size=0;
      _moveFrom._dRoot=nullptr;
    }
    return *this;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::size() const{
    return _size;
  }
  template<typename KEY> set<KEY>::~set(){
    clear();
  }
  template<typename KEY> void set<KEY>::clear(){
    _size=0;
    clearAVLTree(_dRoot);
    _dRoot=nullptr;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::erase(const KEY & _value){
    long delSucc=0;
    _dRoot=removeFromTree(_dRoot,_value,delSucc);
    if(delSucc==1){
      --_size;
    }
    return delSucc;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::insert(const KEY & _value){
    long addSucc=0;
    _dRoot=insertInTree(_dRoot,_value,addSucc);
    if(addSucc==1){
      ++_size;
    }
    return addSucc;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::insert(const set<KEY> & _s2){
    long l2=_s2.size();
    long fR=0;
    for(int i=0;i<l2;++i){
      fR+= insert(_s2[i]);
    }
    return fR;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::erase(const set<KEY> & _s2){
    long l2=_s2.size();
    long fR=0;
    for(int i=0;i<l2;++i){
      fR+= erase(_s2[i]);
    }
    return fR;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::operator+=(const KEY & _value){
    return insert(_value);
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::operator+=(const set<KEY> & _s){
    return insert(_s);
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::operator-=(const KEY & _value){
    return erase(_value);
  }
  template<typename KEY> long set<KEY>::operator-=(const set<KEY> & _s){
    return erase(_s);
  }
  template<typename KEY> KEY set<KEY>::operator[](const long & i) const{
    if((i>-1)&&(i<_size)){
      return avl_access(_dRoot,i);
    }
    KEY irrelevantValue;
    return irrelevantValue;
  }
  template<typename KEY> std::pair<long,KEY>
  set<KEY>::findIK(const KEY & _v,
      const long & upperBoundInsteadOfNegOne) const{
    AVLNode* researcher= _dRoot;
    std::pair<long, KEY> found;
    found.first=-1;
    long discardedLeft=0;
    while( (researcher!=nullptr)&&(found.first==-1)){
      if(_v<researcher->value){
        researcher=researcher->leftChild;
      }
      else{
        if(researcher->value < _v){
          discardedLeft+=researcher->leftCount+1;
          researcher=researcher->rightChild;
        }
        else{
          found.first=discardedLeft+researcher->leftCount;
          found.second=researcher->value;
        }
      }
    }
    if(found.first*upperBoundInsteadOfNegOne==-1){
      found.first=discardedLeft;
    }
    return found;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long
  set<KEY>::find(const KEY & _v,
      const long & upperBoundInsteadOfNegOne) const{
     return findIK(_v,upperBoundInsteadOfNegOne).first;
  }
  template<typename KEY> long
    set<KEY>::upperBound(const KEY & _v) const{
    return find(_v,1);
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL> class map{
  private:
    struct CompPair{
    public:
      KEY k;
      VAL v;
      int operator<(const CompPair& ) const;
    };
    set<CompPair> s;
  public:
    long size() const;
    long erase(const KEY & );
    long erase(const map & );
    long insert(const KEY & , const VAL &);
    long insert(const map &);
    std::pair<long,std::pair<KEY,VAL> >
    findIKV(const KEY & , const long & = 0) const;
    long find(const KEY &, const long & = 0) const;
    long upperBound(const KEY &) const;
    void clear();
    std::pair<KEY,VAL> operator[](const long & ) const;
  };
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  int map<KEY,VAL>::CompPair::operator<(const CompPair& oth) const{
    if(k<oth.k){return 1;}
    return 0;
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  long map<KEY,VAL>::size() const{
    return s.size();
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  long map<KEY,VAL>::erase(const KEY & _k){
    CompPair p;
    p.k=_k;
    return s.erase(p);
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  long map<KEY,VAL>::erase(const map<KEY,VAL>& _m){
    return s.erase(_m.s);
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  long map<KEY,VAL>::insert(const KEY& _k, const VAL& _v){
    CompPair p;
    p.k=_k;p.v=_v;
    return s.insert(p);
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  long map<KEY,VAL>::insert(const map<KEY,VAL>& _m){
    return s.insert(_m.s);
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  std::pair<long, std::pair<KEY,VAL> >
  map<KEY,VAL>::findIKV(const KEY & _k,
  const long & upperBoundInsteadOfNegOne) const{
     CompPair p;
     p.k=_k;
     std::pair<long, CompPair> res=s.findIK(p,upperBoundInsteadOfNegOne);
     std::pair<long,std::pair<KEY,VAL> > retVal;
     retVal.first=res.first;
     retVal.second.first=res.second.k;
     retVal.second.second=res.second.v;
     return retVal;
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  long map<KEY,VAL>::find(const KEY & _k,
    const long & upperBoundInsteadOfNegOne) const{
    CompPair p;
    p.k=_k;
    return s.find(p,upperBoundInsteadOfNegOne);
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  long map<KEY,VAL>::upperBound(const KEY & _k) const{
    return find(_k,1);
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  void map<KEY,VAL>::clear(){
    s.clear();
  }
  template<typename KEY, typename VAL>
  std::pair<KEY,VAL> map<KEY,VAL>::operator[](const long & j) const{
    std::pair<KEY,VAL> res;
    CompPair p=s[j];
    res.first=p.k; res.second=p.v;
    return res;
  }
}

 #ifndef _INCL_NW_CPP
 #define _INCL_NW_CPP
 namespace BF{
   double GLOBAL_EPSILON=0.000000001;
   const char CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR='.';
   const std::string CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR_ST=".";
   const char CONST_THOUSANDS_SEPARATOR=',';
   const std::string CONST_THOUSANDS_SEPARATOR_ST=",";
   int isNumeric(const std::string & s,const long & tolerateSignsInFront = 1){
     long sz=s.length();
     long i=0;
     long numDecPoints=0;
     int res=1;
     if(tolerateSignsInFront){
       while( (i<sz) && ((s[i]=='-')||(s[i]=='+'))){
         ++i;
       }
     }
     while((res==1)&&(i<sz)){
       if(s[i]==CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR){
         ++numDecPoints;
       }
       else{
         if((s[i]!=CONST_THOUSANDS_SEPARATOR)&&((s[i]<'0')||(s[i]>'9'))){
           res=0;
         }
       }
       if(numDecPoints>1){res=0;}
       ++i;
     }
     return res;
   }
   std::string makeItZeroIfNotNumeric(const std::string &s, const long & tolerateSignsInFront = 1){
     if(isNumeric(s,tolerateSignsInFront)){
       return s;
     }
     return "0";
   }
   std::string padded(const long & _x,const long & _d, const std::string &paddingSt=" "){
     // Examples:
     // BF::padded(3,100,"0")=003
     // BF::padded(33,100,"0")=033
     // BF::padded(0,100,"0")=000
     // BF::padded(33,100000,"0")=000033
       long x=_x;
       if(x<0){x*=-1;}
       long d=_d;
       std::string fR="";
       while(d>x){
           fR+=paddingSt;
           d/=10;
       }
       if(x>0){fR+=std::to_string(x);}
       return fR;
   }
   std::string removeASCII10AND13(const std::string &_input,const std::string & _replaceWith=""){
       std::string output;
       long len=_input.length();
       long i=0;
       while(i<len){
           if(( static_cast<long>(_input[i])!=13)&&( static_cast<long>(_input[i])!=10)){
               output+=_input[i];
           }
           else{
             output+=_replaceWith;
           }
           ++i;
       }
       return output;
   }
   std::string cleanSpaces(const std::string & _input, const int & removeAllSpaces=0, const int & remove10And13 = 1){
       // removes double space characters
       // removes leading spaces in string
       std::string input=_input;
       if(remove10And13){input=removeASCII10AND13(_input);}
       std::string output="";
       int spaceBefore=1;
       int spaceNow;
       long len=input.length();
       for(long i=0;i<len;++i){
           spaceNow=0;
           if((input[i]==' ')||(input[i]=='\t')||(input[i]=='\n')||(static_cast<long>(input[i])==13)){
               spaceNow=1;
           }
           if(spaceNow!=1){
               output+=input[i];
               spaceBefore=0;
           }
           else{
               if(spaceBefore!=1){
                   if(removeAllSpaces==0){output+=input[i];}
               }
               spaceBefore=1;
           }
       }
       return output;
   }
   std::string cleanAllSpaces(const std::string &_input){
     return cleanSpaces(_input,1);
   }
   long stringToInteger(const std::string &_s){
     std::string t=cleanSpaces(_s,1);
     long sign=1;
     long pos=0;
     long len=t.length();
     if(len<1){
       return 0;
     }
     long fR=0;
       while((pos<len)&&((t[pos]=='+')||(t[pos]=='-'))){
           if(t[pos]=='-'){
               sign *=-1;
           }
           ++pos;
       }
     long zero=static_cast<long>('0');
     while(pos<len){
       if(t[pos]!=CONST_THOUSANDS_SEPARATOR){
         fR*=10;
         fR+=static_cast<long>(t[pos])-zero;
       }
       ++pos;
     }
     fR*=sign;
     return fR;
   }
   std::string removeNonNumericStart(const std::string & _s){
     std::string res;
     long sz=_s.length();
     int stillOK=1;
     while(stillOK&&(sz>0)){
       --sz;
       if( (_s[sz]>='0')&&(_s[sz]<='9') ){
         res = _s[sz]+res;
       }
       else{
         stillOK=1;
       }
     }
     if(sz<1){return res;}
     stillOK=0;++sz;
     while(stillOK && (sz>0)){
       --sz;
       if( (_s[sz]=='-')||(_s[sz]=='+')){
         res = _s[sz] + res;
       }
       else{
         if( (_s[sz]!=' ')&&(_s[sz]!='\t')&&(_s[sz]!='\n') ){
           stillOK=0;
         }
       }
     }
     return res;
   }
   long stringToIntegerRemoveStart(const std::string& _s){
     return stringToInteger(removeNonNumericStart(_s));
   }
   long stringToIntegerRemoveStartAndEnd(const std::string& _s, long maxInt=1000000){
     long res=0;
     long i=0; long sz=_s.length();
     long zero=static_cast<long>('0');
     if(maxInt<1){maxInt=1000000;}
     while((i<sz)&&((_s[i]<'0')||(_s[i]>'9'))){++i;}
     while((i<sz)&&(_s[i]>='0')&&(_s[i]<='9')){
       res*=10;
       res+=static_cast<long>(_s[i])-zero;
       res%=maxInt;
       ++i;
     }
     return res;
   }
   double stringToDouble(const std::string &_s){
     std::string t=cleanSpaces(_s,1);
     double sign=1.0;
     long pos=0;
     long len=t.length();
     if(len<1){
       return 0.0;
     }
     double fR=0.0;
       while((pos<len)&&((t[pos]=='+')||(t[pos]=='-'))){
           if(t[pos]=='-'){
               sign *=-1.0;
           }
           ++pos;
       }
     double zero=static_cast<double>(static_cast<long>('0'));
     while((pos<len)&&(t[pos]!=CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR)){
       if(t[pos]!=CONST_THOUSANDS_SEPARATOR){
         fR*=10.0;
         fR+=static_cast<long>(t[pos])-zero;
       }
       ++pos;
     }
     if(pos<len){
       // We reached the decimal separator
       double decimalMultiplier=0.1;
       ++pos;
       while(pos<len){
         fR+= decimalMultiplier*(static_cast<double>( (t[pos]))-zero);
         decimalMultiplier*=0.1;
         ++pos;
       }
     }
     fR*=sign;
     return fR;
   }
   std::string eraseTrailingZeros(const std::string &st){
     long len=st.length();
     long pos=len-1;int decimalSeparatorFound=0;
     while((pos>-1)&&(st[pos]=='0')){
       --pos;
     }
     if((pos>-1)&&(st[pos]==CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR)){
       --pos;decimalSeparatorFound=1;
     }
     if(pos==-1){
       return "0";
     }
     std::string output="";
     ++pos;
     for(long i=0;i<pos;++i){
       output+=st[i];
       if(st[i]==CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR){decimalSeparatorFound=1;}
     }
     if(decimalSeparatorFound==0){
       return st;
     }
     return output;
   }
     std::string forceDecimals(const double& _d, const long& nD){
     double d=_d;std::string stSign="";
     if(d<0){d=(-1.0)*d;stSign="-";}
     double modified=d;
     for(long i=0;i<nD;++i){
       modified *= 10.0;
     }
     modified *= 10.0;
     long intVal=static_cast<long>(modified);
     long roundUp=0;
     if(intVal%10>4){roundUp=1;}
     intVal/=10;
     intVal+=roundUp;
     std::string result; int dotPrinted=0;
     long i=0;
     if(intVal==0){
       if(nD<1){
         return "0";
       }
       result="0"+CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR_ST;
       for(long i=0;i<nD;++i){
         result+="0";
       }
       return result;
     }
     if(nD<1){
       return stSign+std::to_string(intVal);
     }
     while(intVal>0){
       result = std::to_string(intVal%10)+result;
       ++i;
       if(i==nD){
         result = CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR_ST+result;
         dotPrinted=1;
       }
       intVal/=10;
     }
     while(i<nD){
       result = "0"+result;
       ++i;
     }
     if(dotPrinted==0){
       result= CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR_ST+result;
     }
     if(result[0]==CONST_DECIMAL_SEPARATOR){
       result = "0"+result;
     }
     return stSign+result;
   }
   std::string double_to_string_withPrecision(const double & d, const long &p){
     std::ostringstream tmp;
     tmp.precision(p);
     tmp<<std::fixed;
     tmp<<d;
     return tmp.str();
   }
   std::string doubleToString(const double &d,const long &precision=19){
     return eraseTrailingZeros(double_to_string_withPrecision(d,precision));
   }
   double round(const double & f, const double & d){
     if(f< -GLOBAL_EPSILON){
       return -round(-f,d);
     }
     double result;
     if(d<-GLOBAL_EPSILON){
       return f;//cannot round to negative number of digits
     }
     long dL= static_cast<long>(d+GLOBAL_EPSILON);
     double multiplier=0.1;
     double shiftedF=f;
     ++dL;
     for(long i=0;i<dL;++i){
       multiplier *= 10.0;
       shiftedF *= 10.0;
     }
     long fForNextDigitInt = static_cast<long>(shiftedF+GLOBAL_EPSILON);
     long nextDigit=fForNextDigitInt % 10;
     if(nextDigit>4){
       fForNextDigitInt += 10;
     }
     fForNextDigitInt/=10;
     return (static_cast<double>(fForNextDigitInt)/multiplier);
   }
   double calculateTax(const std::vector<double>& b, const std::vector<double>& r, double x){
     long len=b.size();
     double tax=0.0;
     long counter=0;
     double prevBarrier=0.0;
     while((x>=prevBarrier)&&(counter<len)){
       if((counter==len-1)||(x<=b[counter])){
         tax+=(x-prevBarrier)*r[counter];
       }
       else{
         tax+=(b[counter]-prevBarrier)*r[counter];
       }
       prevBarrier=b[counter];
       ++counter;
     }
     return tax;
   }

 double calculateTaxTable(const std::vector<double>& b, const std::vector<double>& r, double x){
   long k=static_cast<long>(x/50.0+0.0000001);
   double lb=k*50.0;
   double ub=(k+1)*50.0;
   return 0.5*(calculateTax(b,r,lb)+calculateTax(b,r,ub));
 }
   std::string summaryRow(const std::string& form, const std::string& line, const std::string& desc, const std::string& stValue){
     return "<tr><td>"+form+"</td><td>"+line+"</td><td>"+desc+"</td><td class=\"text-end\">"+stValue+"</td></tr>\n";
   }
   std::string summaryRow(const std::string& form, const std::string& line, const std::string& desc, const double& dValue){
     return summaryRow(form,line,desc,dValue);
   }
 }
 namespace LALG{
   template<typename TTT>
   int rowOperationSwitch(std::vector<std::vector <TTT> >& leftM, std::vector <std::vector <TTT> >& rightM, long i, long j){
       TTT temp;
       long k;
       for(k=0;k<(leftM).size();++k){
           temp=(leftM)[i][k];
           (leftM)[i][k]=(leftM)[j][k];
           (leftM)[j][k]=temp;
           temp=(rightM)[i][k];
           (rightM)[i][k]=(rightM)[j][k];
           (rightM)[j][k]=temp;
       }
       return 1;
   }
   template<typename TTT>
   int rowOperationDivide(std::vector<std::vector <TTT> >& leftM, std::vector <std::vector <TTT> >& rightM, long i,TTT divNum){
       for(long k=0;k<(leftM).size();++k){
           (leftM)[i][k] =  ((leftM)[i][k])/divNum;
           (rightM)[i][k] =   ((rightM)[i][k])/divNum;
       }
       return 1;
   }
   template<typename TTT>
   int rowOperation3(std::vector<std::vector <TTT> >& leftM, std::vector <std::vector <TTT> >& rightM,
                     long i, long j, TTT multNum){
                   //i-th row becomes: old ith- multNum *j-th row
       for(long k=0;k<(leftM).size();++k){
           (leftM)[i][k] -=  (leftM)[j][k] * multNum;
           (rightM)[i][k] -= (rightM)[j][k] * multNum;
       }
       return 1;
   }
   template<typename TTT>
   std::vector<std::vector <TTT> > inverse(std::vector <std::vector <TTT> > mat){
       long dim=mat.size();
       std::vector<std::vector <TTT> > inv;
       std::vector<std::vector <TTT> >zeroMatrix;
       std::vector<TTT> tempZero;
       long i,j;
       tempZero.resize(dim);
       for(long i=0;i<dim;++i){tempZero[i]=0;}
       zeroMatrix.resize(dim);inv.resize(dim);
       for(long i=0;i<dim;++i){
         zeroMatrix[i]=tempZero;
         tempZero[i]=1;
         inv[i]=tempZero;
         tempZero[i]=0;
       }
       for(i=0;i<dim;++i){
           j=i;
           while((j<dim) &&(mat[j][i]==0)){++j;}
           if (j==dim){
               return zeroMatrix;
           }
           if(i!=j){
               rowOperationSwitch(mat, inv, i,  j);
           }
           rowOperationDivide(mat,inv,i,mat[i][i]);
           for(j=0;j<dim;++j){
               if(j!=i){
                   rowOperation3(mat,inv,j,i,mat[j][i]);
               }
           }
       }
       return inv;
   }
   template<typename TTT>
   int rowOperationSwitchSys(std::vector<std::vector <TTT> >& leftM, std::vector <TTT>& rightCol, long i, long j){
       TTT temp;
       long k;
       for(k=0;k<(leftM).size();++k){
           temp=(leftM)[i][k];
           (leftM)[i][k]=(leftM)[j][k];
           (leftM)[j][k]=temp;
       }
       temp=(rightCol)[i];
       (rightCol)[i]=(rightCol)[j];
       (rightCol)[j]=temp;
       return 1;
   }
   template<typename TTT>
   int rowOperationDivideSys(std::vector<std::vector <TTT> >& leftM, std::vector <TTT>& rightCol, long i,TTT divNum){
       for(long k=0;k<(leftM).size();++k){
           (leftM)[i][k] =  ((leftM)[i][k])/divNum;
       }
       (rightCol)[i] =   ((rightCol)[i])/divNum;
       return 1;
   }
   template<typename TTT>
   int rowOperation3Sys(std::vector<std::vector <TTT> >& leftM, std::vector  <TTT>& rightCol,
                     long i, long j, TTT multNum){
       //i-th row becomes: old ith- multNum *j-th row
       for(long k=0;k<(leftM).size();++k){
           (leftM)[i][k] -=  (leftM)[j][k] * multNum;
       }
       (rightCol)[i]  -= (rightCol)[j] * multNum;
       return 1;
   }
   template<typename TTT>
   std::vector<std::vector<TTT> > subMatrix(const std::vector<std::vector<TTT> >& M,
                                            const long& tl_row, const long& tl_col,
                                            const long& numRows,
                                            const long& _numCols=-1){
     std::vector<std::vector<TTT> > res;
     long numCols=_numCols;
     if(numCols<0){numCols=numRows;}
     if(numRows<1){return res;}
     long maxR=M.size();
     if(maxR<1){return res;}
     long maxC=M[0].size();
     if(maxC<1){return res;}
     std::vector<TTT> row;
     row.resize(numCols);res.resize(numRows);
     long m_r,m_c;
     for(long c=0;c<numCols;++c){row[c]=0;}
     for(long r=0;r<numRows;++r){res[r]=row;}
     for(long r=0;r<numRows;++r){
       for(long c=0;c<numCols;++c){
         m_r=tl_row+r;
         m_c=tl_col+c;
         if( (m_r>-1)&&(m_r<maxR) ){
           if((m_c>-1)&&(m_c<maxC)){
             res[r][c]=M[m_r][m_c];
           }
         }
       }
     }
     return res;
   }

   template<typename TTT>
   int copySubMatrix(std::vector<std::vector<TTT> >& M, const std::vector<std::vector<TTT> >& S,
                     const long& tl_row=0, const long& tl_col=0){
     long maxR=M.size();
     if(maxR<1){return 0;}
     long maxC=M[0].size();
     long s_numR=S.size();
     if(s_numR<1){return 0;}
     long s_numC=S[0].size();
     if(s_numC<1){return 0;}
     if(tl_row+s_numR>maxR){return 0;}
     if(tl_col+s_numC>maxC){return 0;}
     for(long r=0;r<s_numR;++r){
       for(long c=0;c<s_numC;++c){
         M[tl_row+r][tl_col+c]=S[r][c];
       }
     }
     return 1;
   }
   template<typename TTT>
   int solve(std::vector <std::vector <TTT> >  Mat, std::vector <TTT> b, std::vector <TTT> &sol){
       //return 0 if no solutions or infinitely many solutions
       long n=Mat.size();
       long i,j;
       TTT helpNum;
       for(i=0;i<n;++i){
           j=i;
           while((j<n) &&(Mat[j][i]==0)){++j;}
           if (j==n){return 0;}
           if(i!=j){
               rowOperationSwitchSys(Mat, b, i,  j);
           }
           rowOperationDivideSys(Mat,b,i,Mat[i][i]);
           for(j=0;j<n;++j){
               if(i!=j){
                   helpNum=Mat[j][i];
                   rowOperation3Sys(Mat,b,j,i,helpNum);
               }
           }
       }
       sol=b;
       return 1;
   }
 }
 #endif </pre>

template <typename TTT> TTT minimum(const TTT&a, const TTT& b){
   if(a<b){return a;}
   return b;
}
template <typename TTT> TTT square(const TTT&a){
   return a*a;
}
std::string removeNonNumeric(const std::string& in){
  std::string out;
  long sz=in.length();
  long i=0;
  while(i<sz){
    if( (in[i]>='0') && (in[i]<='9') ){
      out += in[i];
    }
    ++i;
  }
  return out;
}
std::string substring(const std::string& in, const long& st, const long& en){
  std::string out;
  long sz=in.length();
  long i=st;
  while((i<sz)&&(i<en)){
    out+=in[i];
    ++i;
  }
  return out;
}
[#]IOStructures[/#]
double power(double a, double b){
  return std::exp(b*std::log(a));
}
double totalInterest(const double& t, const double& iR, const double& C, const double& nMonths){
  double rhoP=(iR/12.0)+1.0;
  double res=t*(power(rhoP,nMonths)-1.0);
  res-= C*rhoP*( power(rhoP,nMonths-1.0)-1.0)/(iR/12.0);
  res+=C*(nMonths-1.0);
  return res;
}
void calcPayments(const double& t, const double& iRP, const double& len,
                                     double& totalInt, double& monthly, double& firstMonthInt, double& firstYearInt){
  if(t<0.001){return ;}
  double iR=iRP/100.0;
  if(iR<0.0001){return ;}
  if(len<1.001){return ;}
  double mI=iR/12.0;
  firstMonthInt=t*mI;
  double rhoPN=power(1.0+mI,len);
  monthly=t*rhoPN*mI/(rhoPN-1.0);
  totalInt=monthly*len-t;
  firstYearInt=totalInterest(t,iR,monthly,12);
}
int main(){
  [var]totalInt01;double;2[/var]  [var]monthly01;double;2[/var]  [var]firstMonthI01;double;2[/var]  [var]firstYearI01;double;2[/var]

  [var]totalInt05;double;2[/var]  [var]monthly05;double;2[/var]  [var]firstMonthI05;double;2[/var]  [var]firstYearI05;double;2[/var]

<h4>Make grading easier with custom rules and policies</h4>
_hideReveal__revealTitle_Show details_/revealTitle__hideTitle_Hide details_/hideTitle_
<h5>Adding a rule</h5>
<p>Let us show an example of a custom rule called <code>pineapple</code>. A rule can be added by inserting the command below into the comment
section of a problem that is being graded.</p>
<pre>[add]pineapple;
-3;
<p>Your solution contains a recipe that adds pineapple to a pizza.
This is really bad.
Three points will be deducted from your score.</p>
[/add]</pre>
<p>The rule will be added to a table. The command will disappear from the comment section. </p>
<h5>Applying a rule</h5> <p>You can apply this rule for any of the students. Just write the following in the comment section: </p>
<pre>[r]pineapple[/r]</pre>
<p>The poor student will loose 3 points and receive the feedback specified with the rule.</p>
<h5>Changing a rule</h5>
<p>If you later change your mind, and decide that 5 points should be deducted instead of 3, then you need to add the command: </p>
<pre>[add]pineapple;
-5;
<p>Your solution contains a recipe that adds pineapple to a pizza.
This is really bad.
Five points will be deducted from your score.</p>
[/add]</pre>
<p>All students who were subject to the rule will have their score and the feedback changed.</p>
<h5>Deleting a rule</h5>
<p>If you want to delete a rule, then type the command:</p>
<pre>[delete]pineapple[/delete]</pre>
_/hideReveal_
<p></p>
